<li class="logitem"><a href="#17:00:03" name="17:00:03" class="time">[17:00:03]</a> <span class="person" style="color:#225ee6">&lt;Travis_McCrea&gt;</span> First you must have a bank account before filing that paperwork </li>
<li class="logitem"><a href="#17:00:48" name="17:00:48" class="time">[17:00:48]</a> <span class="person" style="color:#225ee6">&lt;Travis_McCrea&gt;</span> You don't /have/ to have a corporation to get a bank account, but it removes the liability from you. </li>
<li class="logitem"><a href="#17:00:57" name="17:00:57" class="time">[17:00:57]</a> <span class="person" style="color:#225ee6">&lt;Travis_McCrea&gt;</span> It's a non-profit incorporation so it's cheaper than normal </li>
<li class="logitem"><a href="#17:01:59" name="17:01:59" class="time">[17:01:59]</a> <span class="person" style="color:#225ee6">&lt;Travis_McCrea&gt;</span> If you don't have a corporation, then you must put your own name down as the owner of the account which also means that if you fail to jump through every hoop properly -- it's your neck on the line. It also makes it more difficult for you to give access to the account to other people. </li>
<li class="logitem"><a href="#17:02:23" name="17:02:23" class="time">[17:02:23]</a> <span class="person" style="color:#225ee6">&lt;Travis_McCrea&gt;</span> However, if you don't want to do that you don't have to (you can file online for $90, and I think it's $60 to mail in) </li>
<li class="logitem"><a href="#17:03:47" name="17:03:47" class="time">[17:03:47]</a> <span class="person" style="color:#cc749c">&lt;CalebLangeslag&gt;</span> So then how do I get the bank account? Would I just have another 'personal' account, if business or non-profit accounts require registration? </li>
<li class="logitem"><a href="#17:04:48" name="17:04:48" class="time">[17:04:48]</a> <span class="person" style="color:#225ee6">&lt;Travis_McCrea&gt;</span> Again you have two options: You create a business account under your own name, which you can do without filing for incorporation with the state, or you can get incorporation and create a business account under the corporations name </li>
<li class="logitem"><a href="#17:05:54" name="17:05:54" class="time">[17:05:54]</a> <span class="person" style="color:#225ee6">&lt;Travis_McCrea&gt;</span> Normally they will also ask for minutes of the meeting which dubbed you the responsible person for the account, but if you are filing the incorporation paperwork you can put your name as the board and chief agent and stuff and point to that (it's what I did) </li>
